< text>
We really enjoyed this venue for our December wedding. We originally planned to have our ceremony at a different location but we had to change last minute because of the weather but ended up being able to have our ceremony outside on the patio area. The greenery surrounding the patio is nice so we were happy with that backdrop. We had the dinner inside and it was definitely intimate with 56 guests. I'm glad we ended up with that number because with any more people it probably would have felt crowded. The bridal room is very small, we did not use it to get ready, but even with storing some of our bags and other items it was cramped. You have to use an approved caterer. We used Culinary Excellence and they were great! There is not a full kitchen on-site though so they were cooking in a tent out in the parking area. This venue allows beer & wine only, no liquor. The interior and exterior are nice enough on their own so we really didn't need to decorate very much to make it look nice. It's a very nice property considering the low cost to rent.<//text>

We didn’t need a platform for our ceremony because the patio was already surrounded with beautiful natural scenery. the view of the lake was beautiful. <user_id>103475958951888128656< /user_id><user_name>Mark Poirier<//user_name><time>1619719857946<//time><Rating>5<//Rating>< review>
Our lateral line was clogged with “flushable” wipes (turns out NO wipes are flushable, except toilet paper, which completely disintegrates in water).  As a result, we had a sewage backup into “the lowest point above the blockage,” which for us, was the downstairs bathroom, adjacent to our nice wood floors, just off of our living room.  Fun!  We were a wreck.  Then Alberto shows up on the scene, and quickly and methodically got to work “jetting” our “lateral line,” leading from the house out to the main, city, sewer line, out in the street.  Alberto was extremely helpful, sympathetic, and professional.  He patiently explained that, over time, the smooth, interior surface of sewer lateral lines can develop small burrs (or worse, have roots from nearby trees growing into them) which can catch onto things like “flushable” wipes, that make their way down the toilet.  After one wipe snags, the next one snags on top of it, and before long, you have a complete blockage, like ours, and a big mess, that NOBODY wants to deal with, all over your bathroom and nice floors.  Alberto happened to have a wet vac with him and, after instructing me to go pour some bleach onto the mess in the bathroom, so it could start to disinfect the mess while he worked on clearing the main clog, he even vacuumed up the bathroom overflow for us and disposed of it down the toilet.  We were SO THANKFUL for ALBERTO that night, and we wish him and his family, and his two college-age daughters ALL THE BEST.  THANK YOU, ALBERTO!!< /review>

My plumber recommended Magic Plumbing because he doesn't do sewer jobs.  Here's my impression of the operation:

1) Professional:  the receptionist/dispatcher immediately answered my call, walked me through the details of my plumbing issue, and scheduled me for a same day appointment.  Also, I appreciated that the company is available during "off hours" - for those of us with an urgent issue that might arise outside of regular business hours.

2) The repair guys arrived on time.  Even more amazing, they send you a text that shows their exact driving location and expected arrival time (in minutes).  Nice touch.

3) The nature of my issue required two visits.  Marcus came first and was very helpful.  On the second visit Frank did most of the work and was very patient with my questions.  He was really intuitive about knowing what the problem was, having worked for the company for many years.  And he was totally up front about the options available and what the costs would be.  There was no attempt to steer me to the pricier solutions.  Instead, he gave a frank assessment of each option.

4) All told, I highly recommend them and will use them again  (if necessary).<//Text>

<rate>3<//rate>< Text>
I recently had an issue with my sewage ejector pump. On the first visit, Mike came to take a look at the issue. Before Mike's visit, I got a few consultations from other plumbing services, and they all recommended that I replace the entire system. Mike first tried to see whether it is pipes that are clogged. It was a refreshing experience that he didn't immediate jump to replacing the system. Unfortunately, he did find that the pipes were not clogged, and at that point scheduled another appointment to replace the actual pump. A couple days later, Mike brought another person with him to replace the pump. Upon taking the pump out, he realized the issue was not with the pump, but with the fact that the pipes were damaged and was no longer connected. He went out to purchase a replacement joint in order to allow him to saw off the damaged section of the pipe and replace it. He was able to fix the issue, and now the ejector pump is working. The only reason I have this listed at 3-star is price. For the initial visit, I was charged $250, and he spent only 45 minutes to essentially do a diagnostic. He did agree to discount half of it towards the final fix, but then charged $1150 for that (including $50 towards a restocking fee since we didn't use the new pump). I found that quite expensive for ~3 hours of work (the material fee was minimal since we only used a few new pipes).< /Text>

< review>
We have used Magic Plumbing a few times in last five years. They are family owned local business and we liked their services as they seemed to be honest and professional.

Last week, we called them to schedule a visit as our tenant had some issues with a washing machine. As we did not know whether the issue was drain in the building or the washing machine, we needed them to go to the apartment and check.

They were able to schedule a visit quickly which I liked, but i did not really liked the way they handle the case, this time... Basically they asked if they can snake the drain and it will cost $250. I assumed that they already check to make sure that drain was blocked and that was reason they needed to snake it. Since i was not at the apartment, i was not able to fully understand what was going on. But from the previous experience with them, i authorized the work.

But then i found out that basically they did not do any testing before they decided to snake the drain. After they snaked the drain, then they pour the water thru the drain and said it was not the problem....Hmm? Why did they actually test the drain first? I don't quite understand the steps they took. I wished they simply pour some water in the drain to do the simple test before decided to snake the drain. At the end, we paid $250 for something we did not need if they tested the situation first.

So unfortunately i have mixed feeling about this company now after the last visit...<//review>
